msg:The Marriott Hotel's service facilities are better than any B&B. If you drive by car, you can park in the parking lot next to the ticket hall if you don't have a reservation to enter the scenic spot. The hotel will send a tourist car to pick you up. The connection is convenient. You can go to the mountains in seconds with just a pick-up call for meals and trips. Everyone must take the free scenic bus and drive at any time. There is a newly opened spa on the negative 1 floor, hot spring pool and dry steam. You can watch movies and make reservations for a massage! Net mulberry 118 yuan. Breakfast includes freshly squeezed vegetable juices and fruit juices, and the basic styles are available. The food at the hotel's Longshe Chinese Restaurant is very delicious! The price is a bit lower than the so-called "private restaurants" and "Shanxi restaurants" in the surrounding area. Each meal for two people to eat near the hotel costs nearly 300 yuan, while ordering at the hotel's Chinese restaurant only costs 100 per person. The facilities in the deluxe double room are not that new. The bed is a bit soft and the pillows are not comfortable. The pillows are not very comfortable and the comfort is average. The hotel provides a bathtub set. Instead of going to those private B&Bs in the mountains, the Marriott at the foot of the mountain is definitely the first choice. .

msg:This is the first time I reviewed a hotel on Ctrip. I can only say that this hotel is average. Strictly speaking, it does not look like a five-star hotel, let alone a hotel under the Marriott Group. I have stayed in many five-star hotels at home and abroad. Hotels such as Kuala Lumpur, Singapore, Thailand, Jeju Island, etc. I have lived in Shenzhen all year round and I am very aware of the overall level of five-star hotels. The most attractive thing for me to choose to stay at the Wutaishan Marriott Hotel this time is that it is a hotel under the Marriott Group. However, I was quite disappointed after checking in. After all, it was the lowest price. The room types all start at 1,000 yuan, but the overall level of the hotel is definitely not at this level. The price/performance ratio is low. Let me write a review of this hotel from the four aspects of facilities, health, environment, and services.

facility:
1Ô∏è‚É£The facilities are the most dissatisfied part of my review this time. It is also the place with the lowest rating. I gave a very poor rating. As a five-star hotel, the central air-conditioning system of the hotel was not turned on, causing the air-conditioning to be completely disabled during check-in. After being unable to open it, I complained to Ctrip official. After Ctrip official coordinated with the hotel, the hotel said that the leader had notified the engineering depar**ent to turn on the air conditioner. However, the air conditioner control panel in the room did not show a drop in temperature. I could not feel the temperature in the room when it was turned on. It will be very stuffy if you don‚Äôt open the balcony
2Ô∏è‚É£There is a loud noise when the toilet door and bathroom door in the room are opened and closed. I don‚Äôt know if it is the room I am unlucky enough to have this problem or if other rooms also have this problem. I booked a deluxe twin room. I don‚Äôt know. Will a room of the same level be like this? Secondly, there is a loud sound when the door of the cabinet (where cups are placed) is opened.


health:
1Ô∏è‚É£The objective evaluation of hygiene is above average. There are hair strands on the non-slip mats and floors in the bathroom. This is not a big problem. However, as a five-star hotel and a very famous group brand, more attention should be paid to detail work. However, Wutaishan Marriott has more defects in detail work.


Environment: The overall environment of the hotel is good, but the decoration of the room floors is relatively old-fashioned. However, this aspect cannot be used to deduct points from the hotel. There is a small scenic spot and ancient town outside the hotel. The overall appearance of the hotel and the lobby are good.


Serve:
1Ô∏è‚É£The service is generally good. However, when I occasionally call the front desk in the room, no one answers. I don‚Äôt know if it is a hardware problem or a lack of staff.
2Ô∏è‚É£The hotel has a shuttle bus to and from the Wutaishan Visitor Hall. This is a plus point. If you want to go to a street, you can also ask for a shuttle bus to pick you up. You only need to call the hotel phone number. As a hotel in a scenic area, this is also a point that I like personally.

The above is the experience of this stay. I can‚Äôt say that I am satisfied with the hotel. There are good parts and bad parts.
